2. Call `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` (no parameters).

1. **Account data is currently cached** because the live API returned a 429 rate‑limit error. The equity and available balances are therefore based on the most recent snapshot, not a live query.
2. **One short position (`VELVET‑USDT`) is open** but is blocked from adding more short exposure and is flagged as missing TP/SL. The self‑heal routine has already attempted to fix this, but verification that TP/SL were successfully placed is required.

4. **No new buy orders are allowed** because the blocked‑buy list is empty, but the blocked‑sell list contains `VELVET‑USDT`, preventing additional short adds on that symbol.
5. **Rate‑limit handling** is active: the system correctly fell back to disk snapshots and logged the 429, preventing a hard failure.

**Key take‑aways**

- The swarm is actively self‑healing but is currently **degraded** due to pending agents and API rate‑limits.  
- All critical fixes (TPSL, dashboard sync, margin drift) have been applied and verified, but the underlying rate‑limit issue persists and must be addressed to restore full TP/SL protection.  
- Mesh fulfillment is only **20 %** (3/15); the next cycle should focus on completing the pending agents and confirming their health.
